Xiao Yuan not only upgraded me to a sea view room, but also prepared birthday cakes, fruits and yogurt in my room. It felt so warm. I originally planned to stay for one day, but I added another day. It rained a little the next morning. The location of the hotel was convenient to go everywhere. I went to Weihai Park first, then to Liugong Island, and also to Bajie. When I came back in the afternoon, the sky was clear. I went back to the hotel to see the sunset: a ray of setting sun spread in the water, half of the river was rustling and half of the river was red. From a distance, the sea was covered with the setting sun and sparkling. In the sky, several seabirds spread their wings and flew slowly, forming a beautiful picture. The sun continued to sink, the clouds were not as golden as at the beginning, and gradually began to darken. The sea also returned to its dark blue color. The sea seemed unwilling to separate from the sun, and sprinkled the last ray of sunlight on the sky, and the sea surface was sparkling.
It is very pleasant to walk around on the beach or pier behind the hotel in the morning and evening. I am in a hurry to go to Zibo today. If I am not in a hurry, I would like to stay for another day and play on the beach behind the hotel for a whole day, catching sea shells.
